 bharat or china ne mangalvaar ko donon deshon ke bich vivaadit seemaa par shanti kaayam karne ke liye seemaa tantra kii ek ruparekha par hastakshar kiye
 The framework was signed at the end of the 15th round of border talks between the special representatives of the two countries
 bharat-china seemaa par vaastavik niyantran rekha (elesi) se lage kshetra main ghuspaith kii shikaayat milane par is ruparekha ke tahat donon deshon ke videsh karyaalay ek-duusare se sampark karenge
 According to the agreement, "the two sides agreed to establish an executive mechanism to settle major border matters involving peace and harmony in the indo-china border region
" yah tantra donon deshon ke bich paraamarsh or sahyog kii suvidha uplabdh karaayega
 " gyaat ho ki seemaa vaarta ke vishesh pratinidhiyon china ke state counslar dai binggugo or bharat ke rashtriya suraksha salaahkaar shivashankar menon ne apni do dinon kii vaarta somvaar se shuru kii
 The talks to outline the demarcation on the map were scheduled to take place in November last year but the proposed talks on China's objection to the Tibetan spiritual guru Dalai Lama were postponed
 tippaniyan China had objected to the Dalai Lama's participation in the Global Buddhist Conference held in New Delhi, but the Indian government refused to succumb to China's objection
 menon ne haal hi mencima ke sawaal ko ek kathin mudda bataaya tha or spasht kiya ki donon desh teen charnon kii vaarta prakriya ke duusare daur main hai
 In the three phases of the negotiations, the two countries will agree on the principles, the delineation mechanism and finally the boundary line
 donon deshon ke vishesh pratinidhiyon ke bich 15wein daur kii seemaa vaarta kii samaapti par is ruparekha par hastakshar hue
 Under this framework, the foreign offices of the two countries will contact each other on the complaint of infiltration into the area along the Line of Actual Control (LAC) along the india-china border
 samjhaute ke mutabik, "bharat-china seemaa kshetra main shanti or sauhaard banane se jude pramukh seemaa maamalon ko sulajhane ke liye donon paksh ek kaaryakari tantra kii sthapana karne par sahamat hue
 This mechanism will facilitate consultation and cooperation between the two countries
 " Special representatives of the border talks, China's State Counselor Dai Binggugo and India's National Security Advisor Shivshankar Menon started their two-day talks on Monday
 nakshe par simakan kii ruparekha taiyaar karne ke liye yah vaarta pichley saal november main honi thi lekin tibeti aadhyatmik guru dalai lamas par china kii aapatti par prastaavit vaarta sthagit kar di gai
 The comments china ne nai dilli main yojit vaishvik buddha sammelan main dalai lamas ke hissaa lene par aapatti jataai thi lekin bharat sarkaar ne china kii aapatti ke aage jhukne se inkaar kar diya
 Menon had recently described the boundary question as a difficult issue and clarified that the two countries are in the second round of the three-stage negotiation process
 vaarta ke teen charnon main donon desh siddhanton, simakan tantra kii ruparekha banane or antat: seemaa rekha par sahamat honge
 According to the agreement, "the two sides agreed to establish an executive mechanism to settle major border matters involving peace and harmony in the indo-china border region
" yah tantra donon deshon ke bich paraamarsh or sahyog kii suvidha uplabdh karaayega
 " gyaat ho ki seemaa vaarta ke vishesh pratinidhiyon china ke state counslar dai binggugo or bharat ke rashtriya suraksha salaahkaar shivashankar menon ne apni do dinon kii vaarta somvaar se shuru kii
 The talks to outline the demarcation on the map were scheduled to take place in November last year but the proposed talks on China's objection to the Tibetan spiritual guru Dalai Lama were postponed
 tippaniyan China had objected to the Dalai Lama's participation in the Global Buddhist Conference held in New Delhi, but the Indian government refused to succumb to China's objection
 menon ne haal hi mencima ke sawaal ko ek kathin mudda bataaya tha or spasht kiya ki donon desh teen charnon kii vaarta prakriya ke duusare daur main hai

 isse pehle ravivaar ko kareeb 20 logon ne malini ke ghar ke saamne ikattha hokar narebaazi kii
 He was called a Naxalite supporter and accused him that his reporting was tarnishing the image of Bastar and the police here
 haalanki espi rajendra das ne hamaare pratinidhi se phone par kaha, 'shikaayat ke aadhaar par jaanch kii ja rahi he or exiaar darj ho gai he
 'but Malini says that he does not know anything about whether the FIR was actually lodged
 'mujhe collector ne phone kar bharosa zarur diya he ki vah espi se baat karenge or mukadmaa darj kiya jayega par abhi sirf prakriya hi chal rahi he
 ' scrol kii news editor supriya sharma kaa kahana he, 'hamale ke kai ghanton baad tak bhi police ne mukadmaa darj nahin kiya or ham apni sahyogi malini kii suraksha ko lekar frickramand hai
 ' malini ne apni shikaayat main saamaajik ekta manch sanghathan ke do logon manish paarekh auki sanpat jha kaa naam liya he
 Interestingly, Manish is a worker of BJP and Sampat Congress
 saamaajik ekta manch kaa daawa he ki vah naksalwad ke khilaaf logon ko lamaband kar rahaa he or un saare logon kaa virodh kar rahaa he, jo naksaliyon ko samarthan kar rahe hai
 Manish Parekh, founder of the forum says, 'we oppose violence
 loktantr par bharosa karte hai
 Efforts are being made to discredit the work of our organization Ekta Manch
 ' On the other hand, Malini Subramaniam says that these people first threatened her on January 10 and said that she was working for the Naxalites
 tab se lagaataar mujhe pareshaan kiya ja rahaa he
 Now these people are also provoking our neighbors that i am a Naxal supporter, 'malini said
 udhar chhattisgarh main sahaafee pehle hi police ke nishane par hai
 The police have been jailed by local journalists Santosh Yadav and Somaru Nag as pro-naxalites
 in donon kii giraftaar ke khilaaf saikadon patrkaar raipur or jagadalpur main pradarshan kar chuke hai lekin mukhyamantri ke aashwaasan ke baad bhi abhi tak donon ko raahat nahin mili he
 The comments malini subramanyam ne enditivi india se kaha, â€˜ye halaat daraane vaale hai
 The profession of journalists is being challenged in this way
 janavaadee tareeke se aap kisi kaa bhi virodh kar sakate hai lekin kisi ke ghar par hamalaa karnaa or is tarah dhamkaana katai thik nahin he
 It seems that these people also want to scare other journalists who are writing the truth
 â€™ Scroll's news editor Supriya Sharma says, "in such a situation, he is more worried about Malini
 is bare main unhone rajya ke mukhyamantri raman singh ko bhi patr likhe hai lekin ab tak koi jawaab nahin mila he
 ' online news portal scrol dot in ke liye jagadalpur se likhane vaali patrkaar malini kaa kahana he ki unke ghar somvaar subah pathar phenke gaye or unki car kaa pichhlaa sheesha tod diya gaya
 Earlier on Sunday, around 20 people gathered in front of Malini's house and shouted slogans
 unhen naksali samarthak bataaya or un par aarope lagaaya ki unki reporting se bastar or yahaan kii police kii chhavi kharaab ho rahi he
 However, SP Rajendra Das told our representative over the phone, 'investigation is being done on the basis of complaint and an FIR has been registered
 ' lekin malini kaa kahana he ki unhen is bare main kuch pataa nahin he ki exiaar asal main darj hui he
 'the Collector has assured me by calling me that he will talk to the SP and a case will be filed, but the process is still going on
 ' Scroll's News Editor Supriya Sharma says, "even after several hours of the attack, the police did not register a case and we are concerned about the safety of our colleague Malini
 ' In her complaint, Malini has named two people from the Samajik Ekta Manch organization, Manish Parekh and Sampat Jha
 dilachasp he ki manish bijepi or sanpat congress kaa kaaryakarta he

 manch ke sansthaapak manish paarekh kaa kahana he, 'ham hinsa kaa virodh karte hai

 ab ye log hamaare padosiyon ko bhi bhadkaa rahe hai ki main naksali samarthak humâ€™ malini ne kaha

 1984 Petitioners again reach Supreme Court to investigate 186 closed cases of anti-sikh violence
 yachikakarta ne court ko bataaya ki janvari ke aadesh ke baavjood nai SIT ne kaam shuru nahin kiya
 One member has not been appointed yet, so soon to be heard
 chif justise ne kaha ki unhen maamle kii jaankaree he wo is maamle ko dekhenge
 The comments 9 janvari ko 186 band maamalon kii jaanch ke liye supreme court ne ek nai SIT kaa gathan kiya tha
 The report of the Supervisory Panel said that out of 239 cases, 186 were closed without investigation
 court ne kaha tha ki nai SIT main hoicourt ke ritred jaj, vartmaan IPS or ritred IPS honge
 The new SIT set up for this will be retired Justice d Dhingra of the Delhi High Court, retired IPS Rajdeep Singh and current IPS Abhishek Dular
 supreme court ne kaha tha ki esaiti do maheene main states report degi
 But in February, the Center had requested to appoint Navneet Ranjan Vasan in place of Rajdeep Singh
 8 agast tak SIT ko jaanch report daakhil kerani he
 On 6 December 2017, the Supervisory Panel constituted by the Supreme Court submitted a report of 241 cases closed by the SIT to the Supreme Court
 supreme court is report par tay karegaa ki ye maamle phir se khole jaaen yaa nahin
 The court said that if anything happens in the report, then it will order action
 1 sitambar ko 1984 kii sikh virdohi hinsa ke maamle main supreme court ne SIT dwaara chantni ke baad band kiye gaye keson kii chaanbin ke liye supreme court ke do ritair jajon ke suparvijri panel kaa gathan kiya tha
 The panel consists of retired Supreme Court Justice JM Panchal and Justice KS Radhakrishnan
 court ne kaha tha ki jaj paanch sitambar se kaam shuru karenge or teen maheene main report denge
 After looking at the records, the panel had to decide whether the decision to close the case was correct and whether to re-examine these cases
 panel shuruyaat main hi band kiye gaye 199 keson ke alaava 42 anya maamalon kii filon ko dekhegaa
 On 9 January, the Supreme Court constituted a new SIT to investigate 186 closed cases
 suparvijri panel kii report main kaha gaya tha ki 239 maamalon main se 186 ko bina jaanch band kiya gaya
 The court had said that the new SIT will consist of retired High Court judges, current IPS and retired IPS
 iske liye gathit nai esaiti main dilli hoicourt ke ritred jaj justise esen dhingra, ritred ipies rajdeep singh or vartmaan ipies abhishek dulaar honge
 The Supreme Court had said that the SIT would give a status report in two months
 lekin farvari main centre ne rajdeep singh kii jagah navaneet ranjan vaasan ko niyukt karne kii guhaar lagaai thi

 6 disambar 2017 ko supreme court dwaara gathit suparvijri panel ne SIT dwaara band kiye gaye 241 keson kii report supreme court ko saunpi thi
 The Supreme Court will decide on this report whether these cases are reopened or not
 court ne kaha ki agar report main kuch hoga to karrwai ke aadesh denge

 panel main supreme court ke ritred jaj justise jeem paanchal or justise kees radhakrishnan hai
 The court had said that the judges would start work from September 5 and report in three months
